\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{aiDetachAllLogStreams()}{aiDetachAllLogStreams()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{_assimp_8cpp_a8f1fe2e8ccc5f93484098114ae7071bf} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2defs_8h_a7d617d307e656cb6ff315ba71ff958d4}{ASSIMP\+\_\+\+API}} void ai\+Detach\+All\+Log\+Streams (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void}]{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Detach all active log streams from the libraries\textquotesingle{} logging system. This ensures that the logging system is terminated properly and all resources allocated by it are actually freed. If you attached a stream, don\textquotesingle{}t forget to detach it again. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}

\index{aiEnableVerboseLogging@{aiEnableVerboseLogging}!Assimp.cpp@{Assimp.cpp}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{aiEnableVerboseLogging()}{aiEnableVerboseLogging()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{_assimp_8cpp_a54a7485c9422348b2f20adcbd192ed64} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2defs_8h_a7d617d307e656cb6ff315ba71ff958d4}{ASSIMP\+\_\+\+API}} void ai\+Enable\+Verbose\+Logging (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_aaf9b3b6ed742722b3d0bbff0f4621691}{ai\+Bool}}}]{d}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Enable verbose logging. Verbose logging includes debug-\/related stuff and detailed import statistics. This can have severe impact on import performance and memory consumption. However, it might be useful to find out why a file didn\textquotesingle{}t read correctly. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em d} & AI\+\_\+\+TRUE or AI\+\_\+\+FALSE, your decision. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\Hypertarget{_assimp_8cpp_a0724c3df077bbc9fd042e0cdabab8887}\index{Assimp.cpp@{Assimp.cpp}!aiImportFile@{aiImportFile}}
\index{aiImportFile@{aiImportFile}!Assimp.cpp@{Assimp.cpp}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{aiImportFile()}{aiImportFile()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{_assimp_8cpp_a0724c3df077bbc9fd042e0cdabab8887} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{build_2_desktop___qt__6__8__3___min_g_w__64__bit-_debug_2_robot_lib_2libraries_2assimp-5_84_82_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structai_scene}{ai\+Scene}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} ai\+Import\+File (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{build_2_desktop___qt__6__8__3___min_g_w__64__bit-_debug_2_robot_lib_2libraries_2assimp-5_84_82_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+File}{, }\item[{unsigned \mbox{\hyperlink{zlib_2contrib_2minizip_2ioapi_8h_a787fa3cf048117ba7123753c1e74fcd6}{int}}}]{p\+Flags}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Reads the given file and returns its content.

If the call succeeds, the imported data is returned in an \doxylink{structai_scene}{ai\+Scene} structure. The data is intended to be read-\/only, it stays property of the ASSIMP library and will be stable until \doxylink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_a9d360f95be3deb87f40abf25d4c047dc}{ai\+Release\+Import()} is called. After you\textquotesingle{}re done with it, call \doxylink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_a9d360f95be3deb87f40abf25d4c047dc}{ai\+Release\+Import()} to free the resources associated with this file. If the import fails, NULL is returned instead. Call \doxylink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_a512bfa5aca8613168d8c5246e09b3935}{ai\+Get\+Error\+String()} to retrieve a human-\/readable error text. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+File} & Path and filename of the file to be imported, expected to be a null-\/terminated c-\/string. NULL is not a valid value. \\
\hline
{\em p\+Flags} & Optional post processing steps to be executed after a successful import. Provide a bitwise combination of the \doxylink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2postprocess_8h_a64795260b95f5a4b3f3dc1be4f52e410}{ai\+Post\+Process\+Steps} flags. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\doxylink{fwd_8h_a0e5c49dba7ec654cdda5735347c00397}{Pointer} to the imported data or NULL if the import failed. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\Hypertarget{_assimp_8cpp_af490d56092a7cb65c2153cd4eccbf37a}\index{Assimp.cpp@{Assimp.cpp}!aiImportFileEx@{aiImportFileEx}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{_assimp_8cpp_a817c9de800628100cabbbed139caaab8} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{build_2_desktop___qt__6__8__3___min_g_w__64__bit-_debug_2_robot_lib_2libraries_2assimp-5_84_82_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structai_scene}{ai\+Scene}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} ai\+Import\+File\+Ex\+With\+Properties (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{build_2_desktop___qt__6__8__3___min_g_w__64__bit-_debug_2_robot_lib_2libraries_2assimp-5_84_82_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+File}{, }\item[{unsigned \mbox{\hyperlink{zlib_2contrib_2minizip_2ioapi_8h_a787fa3cf048117ba7123753c1e74fcd6}{int}}}]{p\+Flags}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structai_file_i_o}{ai\+File\+IO}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+FS}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{build_2_desktop___qt__6__8__3___min_g_w__64__bit-_debug_2_robot_lib_2libraries_2assimp-5_84_82_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structai_property_store}{ai\+Property\+Store}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{props}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\Hypertarget{_assimp_8cpp_aaefb6530ee2d385f2537a4795f71f381}\index{Assimp.cpp@{Assimp.cpp}!aiImportFileFromMemory@{aiImportFileFromMemory}}
\index{aiImportFileFromMemory@{aiImportFileFromMemory}!Assimp.cpp@{Assimp.cpp}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{aiImportFileFromMemory()}{aiImportFileFromMemory()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{_assimp_8cpp_aaefb6530ee2d385f2537a4795f71f381} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{build_2_desktop___qt__6__8__3___min_g_w__64__bit-_debug_2_robot_lib_2libraries_2assimp-5_84_82_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structai_scene}{ai\+Scene}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} ai\+Import\+File\+From\+Memory (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{build_2_desktop___qt__6__8__3___min_g_w__64__bit-_debug_2_robot_lib_2libraries_2assimp-5_84_82_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Buffer}{, }\item[{unsigned \mbox{\hyperlink{zlib_2contrib_2minizip_2ioapi_8h_a787fa3cf048117ba7123753c1e74fcd6}{int}}}]{p\+Length}{, }\item[{unsigned \mbox{\hyperlink{zlib_2contrib_2minizip_2ioapi_8h_a787fa3cf048117ba7123753c1e74fcd6}{int}}}]{p\+Flags}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{build_2_desktop___qt__6__8__3___min_g_w__64__bit-_debug_2_robot_lib_2libraries_2assimp-5_84_82_2contrib_2zlib_2zconf_8h_a2c212835823e3c54a8ab6d95c652660e}{const}} char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+Hint}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Reads the given file from a given memory buffer,

If the call succeeds, the contents of the file are returned as a pointer to an \doxylink{structai_scene}{ai\+Scene} object. The returned data is intended to be read-\/only, the importer keeps ownership of the data and will destroy it upon destruction. If the import fails, NULL is returned. A human-\/readable error description can be retrieved by calling \doxylink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_a512bfa5aca8613168d8c5246e09b3935}{ai\+Get\+Error\+String()}. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em p\+Buffer} & \doxylink{fwd_8h_a0e5c49dba7ec654cdda5735347c00397}{Pointer} to the file data \\
\hline
{\em p\+Length} & Length of p\+Buffer, in bytes \\
\hline
{\em p\+Flags} & Optional post processing steps to be executed after a successful import. Provide a bitwise combination of the \doxylink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2postprocess_8h_a64795260b95f5a4b3f3dc1be4f52e410}{ai\+Post\+Process\+Steps} flags. If you wish to inspect the imported scene first in order to fine-\/tune your post-\/processing setup, consider to use \doxylink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_af18a83214bad29e8582c7d2ac7be3f14}{ai\+Apply\+Post\+Processing()}. \\
\hline
{\em p\+Hint} & An additional hint to the library. If this is a non empty string, the library looks for a loader to support the file extension specified by p\+Hint and passes the file to the first matching loader. If this loader is unable to completely the request, the library continues and tries to determine the file format on its own, a task that may or may not be successful. Check the return value, and you\textquotesingle{}ll know ... \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A pointer to the imported data, NULL if the import failed.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This is a straightforward way to decode models from memory buffers, but it doesn\textquotesingle{}t handle model formats that spread their data across multiple files or even directories. Examples include OBJ or MD3, which outsource parts of their material info into external scripts. If you need full functionality, provide a custom IOSystem to make \doxylink{namespace_assimp}{Assimp} find these files and use the regular \doxylink{assimp-install_2include_2assimp_2cimport_8h_a5345c1c24a0e4b71fff9b485adb11e00}{ai\+Import\+File\+Ex()}/ai\+Import\+File\+Ex\+With\+Properties() API. 
\end{DoxyNote}
